<div id="review_352610235" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/352610235" />
    <a title="Sarah Elizabeth" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7591340-sarah-elizabeth"><img alt="Sarah Elizabeth" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1328957304p2/7591340.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/352610235?book_show_action=true">Jun 21, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sarah Elizabeth" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sarah Elizabeth" href="/user/show/7591340-sarah-elizabeth">Sarah Elizabeth</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/15852302-grasping-at-eternity">review of another edition</a>


          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Sarah Elizabeth by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/4330534-christina-rodriguez">Christina Rodriguez</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7591340-sarah-elizabeth?shelf=r2r-complete">r2r-complete</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7591340-sarah-elizabeth?shelf=read-2013">read-2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7591340-sarah-elizabeth?shelf=won">won</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer352610235" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6880194049190057059">(Source: I won a digital copy of this book, which I told the author I would review. Thanks to author Karen Amanda Hooper.)<br/>17-year-old Maryah is horrified when armed thugs break into her parent’s home, kill both of her parents and her brother, and put her in a coma. <br/>Struggling to come to terms with what has happened, Maryah goes to live with her Godmother Louise in Sedona, to finish recuperating from her injuries, and to maybe move there permanently as was her mother’s wish.<br/><br/>Although she can’t eve</span>
  <span id="freeText6880194049190057059" style="display:none">(Source: I won a digital copy of this book, which I told the author I would review. Thanks to author Karen Amanda Hooper.)<br />17-year-old Maryah is horrified when armed thugs break into her parent’s home, kill both of her parents and her brother, and put her in a coma. <br />Struggling to come to terms with what has happened, Maryah goes to live with her Godmother Louise in Sedona, to finish recuperating from her injuries, and to maybe move there permanently as was her mother’s wish.<br /><br />Although she can’t ever remember meeting Louise, the whole family acts as if they have known her all her life, and when Louise’s son turns out to be the gorgeous boy that she has dreamed about since her coma, Maryah is even more puzzled.<br /><br />What Maryah doesn’t know is that she is an element. A soul who is reborn after death, and that Nathan – the boy she has been dreaming about, is her soul mate. For some reason, the last time Maryah was reincarnated, she chose to erase her memories, which means she has no memory of Nathan or her previous lives at all.<br />Can Maryah ever remember her past? Can she remember Nathan? And why did she choose to erase?<br /><br /><br />An enjoyable YA love story about reincarnation.<br /><br />I really enjoyed this book, I liked Maryah, and I liked Nathan, and I was hoping all the way through that Maryah would remember and they could be back together. I liked the whole soul-mates thing, and I liked how Nathan held himself back, even though he had been missing her for years.<br />Maryah did have moments where she should probably have asked what people meant when people said things that hinted at the whole reincarnation thing, but she was still grieving so I’ll let her off. I did like the way that Nathan seemed a lot more mature than 18 though, which obviously fitted in well with the rest of the story.<br />The other characters were all very real and likeable, and it really did seem like Maryah had a good support system in her Kindrily.<br /><br />I liked the storyline in this book, and I liked the ‘will she, won’t she?’ regarding Maryah’s memory loss. I was surprised that we didn’t find out why Maryah erased, but maybe that will be covered in the next book. I liked the little twists in that story, and I thought that the whole thing came off as really believable, which is difficult when you’re talking about reincarnation! I did like the little surprise at the end, and I’m looking forward to finding out what happens in the next book.<br />Overall; an entertaining and believable YA romance about reincarnation.<br />7.5 out of 10.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="6880194049190057059" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <div class="left bodycol">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7997908-laura?shelf=books-reviewed-for-readers-favourit">books-reviewed-for-readers-favourit</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer331802524" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11407549690662457129">Grasping at Eternity (The Kindrily) After the brutal murder of her family 17 year old Maryah moves to Sedona to live with her god parents who hide a secret - they are perpetually reincarnated souls with supernatural gifts who have chosen to live all of their lives together. Maryah unaware of the fact that she has known them all for hundreds of years as in her previous life she did the unimaginable, she chose to forget everything.<br/> <br/>For her soul mate Nathan there is nothing more painful than lookin</span>
  <span id="freeText11407549690662457129" style="display:none">Grasping at Eternity (The Kindrily) After the brutal murder of her family 17 year old Maryah moves to Sedona to live with her god parents who hide a secret - they are perpetually reincarnated souls with supernatural gifts who have chosen to live all of their lives together. Maryah unaware of the fact that she has known them all for hundreds of years as in her previous life she did the unimaginable, she chose to forget everything.<br /> <br />For her soul mate Nathan there is nothing more painful than looking at the person you love and knowing that they cannot remember you as they willingly gave up their memories. Despite the pain Nathan must hold it together so he can protect Maryah and the rest of his kindrily and if he’s lucky Maryah might regain her memories. After all, love always perseveres, or does it?<br /> <br />Grasping at Eternity is a beautiful book about the power of love and family. Rather than sticking to pre-made supernatural creatures, Karen has made her own, the Kindrily, reincarnated souls who have the power to remember previous lives and to choose where they end up in their future lives. Hooper has a beautiful and flowing writing style that when mixed with her vivid characters and engaging plot draws you deep into the world of the Kindrily.<br /> <br />Grasping at Eternity is a refreshing change from the overdone storylines about vampires and werewolves that generally dominate this genre. Karen Amanda Hooper is definitely an author to look out for as her original plots and believable characters make all her books that of a five star standard.<br /> <br />Reviewed for readers favourite.</span>

<div id="review_362894672" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/362894672" />
    <a title="Nickle Love" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/853832-nickle-love"><img alt="Nickle Love" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1577986572p2/853832.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/362894672?book_show_action=true">Jul 06, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Nickle Love" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Nickle Love" href="/user/show/853832-nickle-love">Nickle Love</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/853832-nickle-love?shelf=tbr-challenge3">tbr-challenge3</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/853832-nickle-love?shelf=2012-reading-challenge">2012-reading-challenge</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/853832-nickle-love?shelf=2012-paranormal-fantasy">2012-paranormal-fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer362894672" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9248799789105340992">[July 20]<br/><br/>First of all, I would like to thank Karen Amanda Hooper for providing me an epub copy of Grasping at Eternity. I just finished reading this lovely novel. I'll write a decent review after I've gathered my thoughts and emotions. Karen, you are one awesome person. Thank you for introducing me to Nathan and Maryah and the rest of their Kindrily. <3<br/><br/>--------------------------------------<br/><br/>[Aug 6]<br/><br/>The first time I read the synopsis of Grasping at Eternity, I was instantly intrigued with the plot.</span>
  <span id="freeText9248799789105340992" style="display:none">[July 20]<br /><br />First of all, I would like to thank Karen Amanda Hooper for providing me an epub copy of Grasping at Eternity. I just finished reading this lovely novel. I'll write a decent review after I've gathered my thoughts and emotions. Karen, you are one awesome person. Thank you for introducing me to Nathan and Maryah and the rest of their Kindrily. &lt;3<br /><br />--------------------------------------<br /><br />[Aug 6]<br /><br />The first time I read the synopsis of Grasping at Eternity, I was instantly intrigued with the plot. If you had the option to erase or retain your memory, what would you choose? This particularly reminded me of a Doctor Who episode, if I'm not mistaken it was in Season 5 Episode 2, where Amy Pond learned about something she thought was so horrible that she opted to delete the memory of what she just saw. In Maryah's case, she didn't just erase a memory of something that happened a few minutes or hours or days or weeks earlier, but she erased all memory from her past lives.<br /><br />Before I read this, I already had an idea what it's about, so when certain characters were introduced, I already knew who they were in Maryah's life. The big secret is why she chose to erase and why is she being hunted.<br /><br />The story is told in Maryah's fist-person point of view. It focuses on her life as she tries to cope with a great loss and dealing with her weird adoptive family. She doesn't remember anything from her past lives so she has no idea why these people act like they've known her forever. Aside from her, the story is also told Nathan's first-person point of view, where he's constantly thinking about Maryah's safety and well-being. He's heartbroken but he's still hopeful that the love of his life would return to him somehow, even when it is believed to be impossible.<br /><br />I love all the characters! I would find myself smiling as I read and I wished I was part of their Kindrily...or even just their world. This is really a wonderful concept and it's a refreshing change from the usual YA novels. Though there were certain concerns that crossed my mind as I was reading, in regards with <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[the process of being an Elemental or being part of the family of any one who was reincarnated. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> I guess that part is a broad topic to elaborate, maybe we'll get some more info about that in the next book.<br /><br />I do not know if it's just me but I think the story is predictable, I already hava an idea <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[who the mystery villain is, the one Nathan recognized, and I knew about the seer and the baby too. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> The more I am intrigued with what happened in their last life, the one before Maryah erased her memory.<br /><br />If you were an Elemental, what powers would you want to have? It's so hard to choose but I think I'd want Nathan's powers. I can go wherever I want and not worry about transportation or being late. As long as can save time by traversing, I wouldn't need to stop time to accomplish more things. Although that power has its own perks.<br /><br />I gave this book a rating of 4 because I really, really enjoyed reading it and I am super intrigued as to why Maryah opted to delete her memory, why she chose to forget about her soulmate.</span>
  <a data-text-id="9248799789105340992" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_611610631" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/611610631" />
    <a title="Vanessa" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16436828-vanessa"><img alt="Vanessa" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1591923220p2/16436828.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/611610631?book_show_action=true">May 09, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Vanessa" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Vanessa" href="/user/show/16436828-vanessa">Vanessa</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16436828-vanessa?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16436828-vanessa?shelf=kindle-books">kindle-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16436828-vanessa?shelf=netgalley">netgalley</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16436828-vanessa?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16436828-vanessa?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16436828-vanessa?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16436828-vanessa?shelf=part-of-a-series">part-of-a-series</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer611610631" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4338882908957978918">ARC provided by the Publisher via NetGalley in exchange for an honest review:<br/><br/>“If you love someone, put their name in a circle; because hearts can be broken, but circles never end.” -Anonymous<br/><br/>Maryah and Michael had the perfect family; a mom and dad who were madly in love, both with them and each other. Everything is as it should be until one night, tragedy strikes and Maryah not only lives through it, but thanks to her gift of memory, she remembers it all…especially him.<br/><br/>“No, death is a gorgeous m</span>
  <span id="freeText4338882908957978918" style="display:none">ARC provided by the Publisher via NetGalley in exchange for an honest review:<br /><br />“If you love someone, put their name in a circle; because hearts can be broken, but circles never end.” -Anonymous<br /><br />Maryah and Michael had the perfect family; a mom and dad who were madly in love, both with them and each other. Everything is as it should be until one night, tragedy strikes and Maryah not only lives through it, but thanks to her gift of memory, she remembers it all…especially him.<br /><br />“No, death is a gorgeous movie-star angel man that rides a motorcycle and sat beside you at the hospital.”<br /><br />Maryah doesn’t know why and honestly thinks she’s gone a little crazy when she moves to Sedona to live with her godmother, Louise, and family. Everyone acts as though they’ve known her forever, claiming her as family; talking about people Maryah has never even met…and Nathanial. Nathanial is Louise’s son and in this lifetime (same as every life before) he’s Maryah’s soul mate, her twin flame. Of course she doesn’t know that. Having not even met him yet, she’s dreamt of him many times. It’s not until a trip to Colorado when she comes face to face with her angel of death; the feelings are so overwhelming she passes out. But remember him, them together, she does not. Maryah has erased; she chose at the end of her last life to forget. She’s a clean slate and Nathanial is devastated.<br /><br />“That was a soul-shattering issue. I saw nothing inside her. No flicker of the depthless light in her eyes, no trace of the soul I had loved for centuries. She had let go of our eternity, and I couldn’t stop grasping onto the memory of who she used to be.”<br /><br />So, how do you make someone who has an uncanny ability to remember everything, remember something or someone she has chosen to forget? Despite their efforts and heartbreak, all a girl really needs is her mother…and someone who can relay the message. <br /><br />“Every soul is a story shelved away in an infinite library in the sky.”<br /><br />This book started out slow with a lot happening and too many different characters to keep track of. There was terminology that I had to “figure out” because they pertain to the story (not the dictionary) which made it hard to follow. Once I got past all of that, everything seemed to just click. It flowed beautifully (even with a constant change in POV), I truly didn’t want it to end. The tale of soul mates and past lives is absolutely fascinating—lovers who transcend lifetimes and continuously seek one another out is the epitome of romance. I’m a sucker for an epic romance. I love that Nathanial and his family fought so hard for Maryah to come back to them as she had been in previous lives. I liked the element of suspense coming from someone wanting to destroy connections and use these ancient gifts to their evil advantage. I loved how the end comes full circle in a sense…it was magical, mystical, heartbreaking and renewing all in one. I cannot wait for the next book: Taking Back Forever due out this year. <br /><br />**4 Soul-Saving Stars**<br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer12002629787725871050">This book i could not put down and I finished in one day but I had no computer to write a review with so I had to wait till It got fixed. Like I said I spent the whole day reading this book I wanted more I didn’t want it to finish, and when it finished I was greatly satisfied with the ending that will hold me till the second part comes out and I cannot wait for that…<br/><br/>Maryah is a 17 year old girl whos life is suddenly turned upside down when two men come into her home and murder her whole family l</span>
  <span id="freeText12002629787725871050" style="display:none">This book i could not put down and I finished in one day but I had no computer to write a review with so I had to wait till It got fixed. Like I said I spent the whole day reading this book I wanted more I didn’t want it to finish, and when it finished I was greatly satisfied with the ending that will hold me till the second part comes out and I cannot wait for that…<br /><br />Maryah is a 17 year old girl whos life is suddenly turned upside down when two men come into her home and murder her whole family leaving her for dead, while she is laying there dying she sees the face of this gorgeous guy and she thinks he is there to take her from this world she thinks he is the angel of death. Then she has to move with her Godmother Louise and this is a slow adjustment as she is getting used to the fact that she has no family and now she has to get used to a whole new family. But Louise and her family are very easy to get along with and they welcome her with open arms and she doesn’t understand why they go to so much effort with her when they hardly know her. She makes new friends and every night she has dreams and the angel of death that she calls him is in her dreams . Then she is invited to Louises son’s birthday and she meet Nathaniel Louise’s son, but the problem is he is the one she saw when she was dying ( her angel of death), he is the one in her dreams, how is that possible. And things progress from here .<br />Slowly she gets told her history that she is a Element. Elements are exceptional souls who are created and gifted to the world in pairs (soulmates) and that Nathaniel is her soulmate and the have spent many past lives together until the last life when she chose to erase. So she doesn’t remember anything of her past lives. Then something happens that slowly triggers her memory and she starts remembering things, about her previous lives and especially about Nathan, how much they loved each other. Meanwhile all this time Nathaniel had started to accept the fact that she was truly gone that she would never remember and it truly was breaking his heart, he felt like she was gone forever that he now had to wonder his lifetimes alone ,but then she does he world is whole again..<br />I have always loved the soulmate concept so I loved this book.. It was an emotional rollercoaster from start to end, you really feel what Nathaniel and Maryah are going through, especially when Nathaniel see’s Mayrah with another guy his heart breaks and I cryed LOL. Karen Amanda Hooper is great author and I cannot wait to read her next instalment of this awesome book. I would recommend this book to anyone..<br /></span>

<div id="review_336526734" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/336526734?book_show_action=true">May 25, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Once" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Once" href="/user/show/3515991-once">Once</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer336526734" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer408455547881095963">Maryah Woodsen is just like any other seventeen year old girl. She believes she is just an ordinary American teenager with no special qualities. Her world quickly spins out of control when she finds her family has been murdered and has their killers standing over her as she tries to run for her life. In what she believes to be a hallucination as she is passing out from being attacked she comes face to face with her "angel of death" as she refers to him. She has no idea that this "angel of death"</span>
  <span id="freeText408455547881095963" style="display:none">Maryah Woodsen is just like any other seventeen year old girl. She believes she is just an ordinary American teenager with no special qualities. Her world quickly spins out of control when she finds her family has been murdered and has their killers standing over her as she tries to run for her life. In what she believes to be a hallucination as she is passing out from being attacked she comes face to face with her "angel of death" as she refers to him. She has no idea that this "angel of death" is really Nathaniel Luna, an Element, who is anything but normal eighteen year old boy who was placed in this world as her soul mate centuries ago. The problem is, Nathaniel is wounded to the center of his soul because his soul mate, Mary (the now seventeen year old Maryah) decided a lifetime ago to erase not only himself but all of their kindrily from her memories. She chose to be reborn to the world without knowing any of them. Nathan will stop at nothing to find Dedrick, the Nefarioun behind the attack on Maryah and her family. Dedrick holds the answer to why Maryah chose to erase after her last life and Nathan desperately needs to find out why.<br /><br />The first word that came to mind as I started reading this book was "refreshing". I could not put this book down. From page 1 to page 391 I was sucked in and did not want to put the book down. Karen Amanda Hooper weaves a very refreshing tale putting a new spin on the classic star crossed love story. Set within this beautiful and at times painful love story are a cast of characters as vibrant as the colors described in the pages of the book. They jump off the page and command your attention. I found myself very invested in the cast of characters and each of their abilities as they try to restore Maryah's memories. <br /><br />I'd recommend this story to anyone who loves a really beautiful love story and wants to hear it told from a new perspective. If the love story doesn't draw you in, read it for the lore that she builds this story around. I loved this book and personally can not wait for the sequel in 2013!</span>
  <a data-text-id="408455547881095963" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_353033737" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/353033737" />
    <a title="Naomi" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7993053-naomi"><img alt="Naomi" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1374034636p2/7993053.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/353033737?book_show_action=true">Jun 21, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Naomi" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Naomi" href="/user/show/7993053-naomi">Naomi</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer353033737" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4213989649400055114">Loved it, loved it, loved it!!<br/><br/>Karen Amanda Hooper gave me the opportunity to read her book and in return I was to give her book a review, so obviously I snapped her up on it. I'm not the kind of person to give big reviews because I don't see the point of rewriting the story for you, especially because the writer has done a better job already. <br/><br/>So, if you read the first chapter of 'Grasping At Eternity' and are not drawn into it from the  very beginning, well the book just isn't for you. But to me</span>
  <span id="freeText4213989649400055114" style="display:none">Loved it, loved it, loved it!!<br /><br />Karen Amanda Hooper gave me the opportunity to read her book and in return I was to give her book a review, so obviously I snapped her up on it. I'm not the kind of person to give big reviews because I don't see the point of rewriting the story for you, especially because the writer has done a better job already. <br /><br />So, if you read the first chapter of 'Grasping At Eternity' and are not drawn into it from the  very beginning, well the book just isn't for you. But to me, I was hooked from that first chapter and was left in a bit of shock because I didn't expect something like that to happen straight up! From that moment, I just could not put it down!!<br /><br />Karen has written a fantastic story about Soul Mates and explored reincarnation on a different level. To be able to remember all your past lives and have some supernatural abilities to go along with it.... Simply fabulous! Also, throw in the bad guys who want you to join them or you will die, it just screams fun!!<br /><br />It has a great romantic storyline and has been written from two POV's, Maryah and Nathaniel, and it has been done to perfection. To see both sides of these Soul Mates, knowing that Maryah has erased her previous lives from memory and is finding it hard to rebuild her life with her new family, while Nathaniel is finding it difficult to be around Mariyah  and is unable to believe that she can recover her memories.<br /><br />As it is the first book in the series, Maryah and Nathaniel's journey in this life has only just began. I have so many questions that have been left unanswered, so I can't wait for the next book in the series, Taking Back Forever, expected to release in early 2013.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="4213989649400055114" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_464850012" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/464850012" />
    <a title="JeanBookNerd" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5519230-jeanbooknerd"><img alt="JeanBookNerd" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1560846178p2/5519230.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/464850012?book_show_action=true">Nov 27, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="JeanBookNerd" class="user" itemprop="url" name="JeanBookNerd" href="/user/show/5519230-jeanbooknerd">JeanBookNerd</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5519230-jeanbooknerd?shelf=reviews">reviews</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer464850012" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1155634742640259616">Karen Amanda Hooper’s first book in the Kindrily Series, Grasping at Eternity, tells the interesting story of seventeen-year-old Maryah Woodsen. After a brutal attack that left her parents and twin brother dead with the attacker leaving her barely alive, Maryah must recover with the feeling of her whole world being shattered. She’s sent off to live with her godmother and her family who has a deep dark secret – they are reincarnated souls with supernatural abilities. During these times, peculiar </span>
  <span id="freeText1155634742640259616" style="display:none">Karen Amanda Hooper’s first book in the Kindrily Series, Grasping at Eternity, tells the interesting story of seventeen-year-old Maryah Woodsen. After a brutal attack that left her parents and twin brother dead with the attacker leaving her barely alive, Maryah must recover with the feeling of her whole world being shattered. She’s sent off to live with her godmother and her family who has a deep dark secret – they are reincarnated souls with supernatural abilities. During these times, peculiar dreams of a handsome man with green eyes keeps her mind occupied at night. To make matters worse, her adoptive family is not the best, almost showing an unwelcoming feeling towards her presence in their home. Maryah can’t blame them for feeling that way since they barely know her…or so she thinks.<br /><br />It is obvious that power of love and family are the focal point of this story. Author Karen’s puts her own twist into a family with supernatural gifts, calling them the Kindrily who are reincarnated souls with the ability to remember previous lives. Karen’s writing style is filled with rich descriptions of a family with century old secrets. The characters are vividly alive and engage in situations that make the plot progress and readers will find themselves engulfed into the world of the Kindrily. Once readers are mesmerized by this wonderful world, they will have a difficult time finding the exit door. Grasping at Eternity is an amazing and refreshing idea of a family with a unique lifestyle. Karen has delivered an original plot with likable characters living in a well-thought-out world. Its uniqueness is admirable and will definitely not disappoint.</span>
  <a data-text-id="1155634742640259616" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer692579451" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16671268331589790196">Grasping at Eternity by Karen Amanda Hooper Grasping at Eternity gave me everything I wanted out of this book and more! If I wasn't already a huge fan of novels about Reincarnation, Grasping at Eternity would make me one. Karen Amanda Hooper adds some twists to the idea that really add to the story and helped keep me interested.The characters are all vibrant and all have very different personalities. I fell in love with them and really enjoyed finding out more about their past lives. Reading abo</span>
  <span id="freeText16671268331589790196" style="display:none">Grasping at Eternity by Karen Amanda Hooper Grasping at Eternity gave me everything I wanted out of this book and more! If I wasn't already a huge fan of novels about Reincarnation, Grasping at Eternity would make me one. Karen Amanda Hooper adds some twists to the idea that really add to the story and helped keep me interested.The characters are all vibrant and all have very different personalities. I fell in love with them and really enjoyed finding out more about their past lives. Reading about their past lives got a bit confusing at times, but it made sense for it to be that way. They can't control what body they are reborn into. One life your best friend may be reborn as your brother/sister, the next they may be your father/mother! The one constant is they always had their soulmates. Until Marayah went and screwed that up for Nathan by Erasing that is.Grasping at Eternity was a wonderful blend of just about everything I love in a story. Romance, Action, history, fantasy and a bit of mystery! I cannot wait to read book #2 and see what happens. Grasping at Eternity left me with my heart racing and dying to know what happens next. I also plan for sure on reading Karen Amanda Hooper's other book  Tangled Tides. I'm curious to see what more this author has to offer and what she does in the world of Mermaids!<br /> <br />To read more of my reviews please visit <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://thepassionatebookworm.blogspot.com">http://thepassionatebookworm.blogspot...</a> !</span>

<div id="review_1569097026" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1569097026" />
    <a title="☆☆Hannah☆☆" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12469968-hannah"><img alt="☆☆Hannah☆☆" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1602815563p2/12469968.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1569097026?book_show_action=true">Mar 04, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="☆☆Hannah☆☆" class="user" itemprop="url" name="☆☆Hannah☆☆" href="/user/show/12469968-hannah">☆☆Hannah☆☆</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/15852302-grasping-at-eternity">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1569097026" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8430457017960737491">This was another book with a terrible main character. Maryah tells Nathan that she wants to die. She even tells him that she prays to die everyday. He wants to show her that she doesn't feel that way. So he does something and unfortunately it backfires and they really do almost die. She then starts screaming at him and calls him a psycho for most of the book. Really? You tell him that you want to die and you almost do then YOU call him names. Her stupidity was just too much for me. </span>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_286146778" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/286146778" />
    <a title="Heather McCorkle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4366250-heather-mccorkle"><img alt="Heather McCorkle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1395503652p2/4366250.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/286146778?book_show_action=true">Feb 29, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Heather McCorkle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Heather McCorkle" href="/user/show/4366250-heather-mccorkle">Heather McCorkle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer286146778" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8302273977335279011">This novel is an outstanding sojourn into what it means to truly love and the depths of sacrifice one will go to for that love. I haven't read an opening this gripping since Across The Universe by Beth Revis. Once Grasping At Eternity had me in its grip, it never let me go. The stars will always seem brighter to me now. <br/><br/>Highly Recommend!!!</span>

          </span>
        </div>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('w+V1hKFz53lTU/kmjztRxELjkoBmqePP2fTpb+qh+weoVKoyg1T6dg5fuzHr0TJ1qmGceByQ1ld7Z1rTJan2+A==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('VhWousktP7VgIaHoQkCMrXpGt36TznQAi4PnRWbnkW09pHcM6woiuj0t4/8mqu8cksS5hun3QZgpEFT5qe+ckg==')})
  }
